dict tree:
One day in json '[]'
    lat 
    longitude
    timezone
    'Hourly':
        summary
        icon
        'data':
            [list 24 dicts, each dict is one hourly update]
                dict:
                    Unix time:
                    summary
                    icon
                    precipIntensity
                    precipProbability
                    temperature
                    apparentTemperature
                    dewPoint
                    humidity
                    pressure
                    windSpeed
                    windGust
                    windBearing
                    cloudCover
                    uvIndex
                    visibility
    'daily':
        'data':
            [{unixtime(12am that day):
            summary
            icon
            sunriseTime
            sunsetTime
            moonPhase
            precipIntensity
            precipIntensityMax
            precipIntensityMaxTime
            precipProbability
            precipType
            temperatureHigh
            temperatureHighTime
            temperatureLow
            temperatureLowTime
            apparentTemperatureHigh
            apparentTemperatureHighTime
            apparentTemperatureLow
            apparentTemperatureLowTime
            dewPoint
            humidity
            pressure
            windSpeed
            windGust
            windGustTime
            windBearing
            cloudCover
            uvIndex
            uvIndexTime
            visibility
            temperatureMin
            temperatureMinTime
            temperatureMax
            temperatureMaxTime
            apparentTemperatureMin
            apparentTemperatureMinTime
            apparentTemperatureMax
            apparentTemperatureMaxTime
    offset (minus hours to get local timezone)
